## By domain

- [go to top](#wikimedia-readiness-for-digital-maryland)

1. '[**collections.digitalmaryland.org**](https://collections.digitalmaryland.org)' *(e.g. '[Maryland State Archives](https://dp.la/search?provider=%22Maryland+State+Archives%22&partner=%22Digital+Maryland%22)')* has a **very high** readiness score because it has **22,549** eligible public domain items (**11%** of **196,987** total items) across all collections hosted on this domain in CONTENTdm, and **1,829** additional items over 120 years old in other rights categories that could become eligible with rights review.
